Please separate the coreference words by commas in the output.<n><n>### Input:<n>The CEO reminded the housekeeper to sweep up because she often forget.<n><n>### Response:<n>		The CEO remindedthe housekeeper to sweep up since she often forget.

Machine comprehension of unstructured, real-world text is a major research goal for natural language processing. Current tests of machine comprehension pose questions whose answers can be inferred from some supporting text, and evaluate a model’s response to the questions. The EpiReader is an end-to-end neural model comprising two components: the first component proposes a small set of candidate answers after comparing a question to its supporting text, and the second component formulates hypotheses using the proposed candidates and the question, then reranks the hypotheses based on their estimated concordance with the supporting text. We present experiments demonstrating that the EpiReader sets a new state-of-the-art on the CNN and Children’s Book Test machine comprehension benchmarks, outperforming previous neural models by a significant margin.<n><n>### Response:<n>		A novel model for machine comprehension offers promising results in the discovery of anchoring text.
